23 mins: Discussion and Brainstorming session with Experts and other Entrepreneurs. 

*Observer*

*What is this partnership all about?*
GMI will be assessing YOU and your MANAGERS via a short survey sent to all your employees once you REGISTER.

*Whats the Criteria for Qualification?* 
1) Any individual who has minimum 3 or more team members is eligible for individual recognition: TOP 100 Great People Managers. 

2) Any organization who has more than 50 employees and has operations in India for than 2 years is eligible for organizational recognition: TOP 50 Organizations. 

And both are not mutually exclusive, one individual can feature as well as his organization (if eligible) and vice versa. ;) ;)

[17/01/19, 10:02:47 AM] â€ª+91Â 91670Â 44053â€¬: We talk about relationships in sales business development. Some people just mix it with bad ideas of getting closer with hidden  agenda of getting / selling something  long chatting talking..coffe etc few of those tricks. Basically rubbing the other one to the point he gets irritated to throw some kind of forced deals that mostly not gets materialized due to its sheer onesided less interested throw away nature.

The real relationship kick starts immediately when you first give something to the other one again and again instead of asking sly return first. 

The law of attraction says do it 4 times. 

I have experimented this too. Even before i ask for something offer has been poured in to me. Offer someone your skills, expertise, experience free of cost. And see what happens. 

Those who into sales try it out. You are not able to sell because you are trying to force your way to sell. Instead pls be genuine to help and offer values and seek nothing in return. You need not to ask, things will come back to you in multitudes of what you offered free.

#mythoughts #youmightbedifferent #genuinesales

[01/02/19, 1:49:42 PM] Rajesh Khemani(ps): No tax upto total taxable Income of 5Lakh is in the form of rebate under section 87A which means *It will be available to only those Individuals whose Total Taxable Income is less than or equal to 5Lakh (after availing all available deductions).*

*There is no change in Tax slabs and there is no exemption to those Individuals whose total Taxable Income (after all deductions) is more than 5Lakh.*

[01/02/19, 1:59:22 PM] Nishant (Beingjigyasu): No. That's the catch. It's doubled for only those whose income after deductions comes below or equal to 5 Lakhs. 

E.g. if someone earns 6.5 Lakhs and invests in tax saving instruments upto 1.5 Lakhs (upper limit of 80C), then the individual doesn't have to pay any tax at all.

But if you earn more than that or you're unable to bring post deduction income to 5 lakhs or less, then the 2.5 Lakh slab and 5 Lakh slabs remains as is.

Exeprt from this article

_This can be further explained as follows. If your net taxable income after availing all the deductions under section 80C to 80U of the Income tax act does not exceed Rs 5 lakh, then you will not be required to pay any tax. However, if your net taxable income (after availing deductions under section 80C to 80U), exceeds Rs 5 lakh then taxes will be calculated as per the current tax structure._

[25/02/19, 11:06:07 PM] â€ª+91Â 73037Â 55692â€¬: *Registered Office KYC*

Ministry of Corporate Affairs has taken a new step to identify the Active Companies and to verify their Registered Office.So now every company need to do Registered office KYC.

*Rule*
Rule 25A (Companies Incorporation amendment ) Rules 2018

Applicable on Every Company Incorporated on or before 31/12/2017.

*Form:*
Form INC-22A (ACTIVE- Active Company Tagging Identities and Verification)

*Basic Information or documents required*

1. Email id of company (on which OTP will come)
2. Provide latitude and longitude of the Regd office.
3. Photographs of Regd Office showing external building and inside office also showing therein at least one director who has affixed his/her Digital Signature to this form.


*Due date - On or before 25-04-2019*

If any Company fails to file Active Form on or before 25 April 2019 than Such Company marked as Non Compliant Company by MCA.

*Late fee - After due date Rs. 10,000.*

[07/03/19, 11:36:20 AM] Bharat Jethani (ps): After a meeting or chat, itâ€™s often useful to document the agreed actions. This gives everyone clarity on next steps. Itâ€™s also a useful audit trail for us.

Hereâ€™s a follow-up email that works wellâ€¦

Subject: Our actions following todayâ€™s meeting. Please can youâ€¦

Dear (Name)

I enjoyed our meeting.

As promised, this email confirms the actions we agreed.

My actions:

     
      
Yours:

      
If Iâ€™ve missed anything, please let me know.

As agreed, weâ€™ll meet again at (time) on (date), to finalise our next steps.

This wording works well because:

The title engages â€“ â€œplease can youâ€¦â€ encourages them to open the email â€“ they want to see what the second half of the sentence is
The wording is very joint â€“ â€œour meetingâ€ and so on
The word â€œagreedâ€ reinforces weâ€™ve agreed things
Weâ€™ve both got actions â€“ so itâ€™s joint and fair
You put your actions before theirs
Youâ€™ve documented when youâ€™re meeting again. So things happen with pace
Most of all: itâ€™s better than NOT sending one. That makes things go too slowly. Or not at all.

Action Point

Create a standard follow-up email (or just use this one). You can then use it after every meeting â€“ a quick way to get more done.
